<script type="text/javascript" nonce="OSwxMTU=">window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
function fetchResults(){
    var keyword = jQuery('#busqueda').val();
    if(keyword == ""){
        jQuery('#datafetch').html("");
    } else {
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: 'https://www.cialdnb.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
            type: 'post',
            data: { action: 'data_fetch', keyword: keyword  },
            success: function(data) {
                jQuery('#datafetch').html( data );
            }
        });
    }
    

}
});</script>
